);

CREATE TABLE [Member] (
    [rowid] integer PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT NOT NULL,
    [component_id] integer NOT NULL,
    [type] string NOT NULL,
    [arrow_dir] integer NOT NULL DEFAULT -1,
    [choice] integer NOT NULL,
    [layer] integer NOT NULL,
    [x] integer NOT NULL,
    [y] integer NOT NULL,
    [element_type] integer NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
    [element] integer NOT NULL DEFAULT 0
);

CREATE TABLE [Component] (
    [rowid] integer PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT NOT NULL,
    [level_id] string,
    [type] string NOT NULL,
    [x] integer NOT NULL,
    [y] integer NOT NULL,
    [name] text DEFAULT NULL,
    [active_layers] integer NOT NULL DEFAULT 200,
    [visible_layers] integer NOT NULL DEFAULT 255,
    [locked_layers] integer NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
    CONSTRAINT [FK_Component_0] FOREIGN KEY ([level_id]) REFERENCES [Level] ([id])
);

CREATE TABLE [ResearchNet] (
    [level_id] text PRIMARY KEY NOT NULL,
    [when_created] datetime NOT NULL,
    [definition] text NOT NULL
);
CREATE TABLE [Level] (
    [id] string PRIMARY KEY NOT NULL,
    [passed] bit NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
    [mastered] bit NOT NULL,
    [cycles] int NOT NULL,
    [symbols] int NOT NULL,
    [reactors] int NOT NULL,
    [best_cycles] integer NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
    [best_symbols] integer NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
    [best_reactors] integer NOT NULL DEFAULT 0
);
